into revenue
Transform every sales call into actionable insights for coaching and productivity. Automate call reviews, close skill gaps with targeted training, keep CRM up-to-date and more.

1. Capture
2. Coach
3. Practice
1. Capture
2. Coach

Step 1 — Capture
Capture real-life **performance** and **insights** by analyzing 100% of calls with **AI trained on your process**. Use our Bot or call recording integrations.

## What Makes UserMotion Unique?
Quick to set up, simple to use, and with numerous integrations. But there’s more. Explore some of our features and capabilities.
##### Predictive Lead Scoring
Predictive Lead Scoring algorithm identifies high-potential leads and ranks them based on buying signals, product usage data, Ideal Customer Profile Score, and more.
##### ICP Matching
UserMotion enhances your targeting strategy by precisely matching leads with your Ideal Customer Profile (ICP), ensuring you focus your efforts on the prospects most likely to convert and grow with your solution.​
##### PQL Scoring​
UserMotion's PQL (Product Qualified Lead) Scoring algorithm identifies high-potential leads directly within your product usage data, enabling targeted engagement that maximizes conversion opportunities.
##### Customer Health Score
Customer 360 provides actionable insights and a Customer Health Score from customer interactions, encouraging proactive engagement, lowering churn, and building long-term relationships.
##### Expert Made Playbooks
Our Expert-made Playbooks are created using industry best practices to provide actionable step-by-step guidance to your GTM teams to engage customers and maximize conversion rates.
##### Enterprise-Grade Security
We protect your data with SOC 2 Type II compliance, regular security audits, and strict GDPR readiness. Single Sign-On simplifies access while customizing permissions.

Platform
## The only all-in-one sales engagement platform with built-in lead management and auto dialer
Vanillasoft is the only sales engagement platform that includes the orchestration and automation of calls, emails and SMS; powerful auto dialing software; and lead management software. We’re an all-in-one tool, with no swivel chair or platform switching. 
![people around a conference table](https://vanillasoft.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcdn.sanity.io%2Fimages%2Fc35pm3dk%2Fproduction%2Ffb853f7568305207ac56fb1d00d92a5ad4fcda82-1920x1080.jpg%3Fauto%3Dformat&w=3840&q=75)
###  Lead Management
Vanillasoft’s lead management tools push the next best record in real time so agents don’t waste time figuring out their next lead to contact. Top records are always worked first, so the most valuable records aren’t wasted. 
Native to our sales engagement platform
The best leads are orchestrated for next contact in outreach and automated cadences
Less busy work and improved agent productivity and effectiveness 
[Learn more](https://vanillasoft.com/platform/lead-management)
![woman at a desk smiling with a headset](https://vanillasoft.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcdn.sanity.io%2Fimages%2Fc35pm3dk%2Fproduction%2F70f932e6c60c001c2bde60ab35686e98dd4505c2-1920x1080.jpg%3Fauto%3Dformat&w=3840&q=75)
###  Auto Dialer
Vanillasoft’s auto dialer software balances agent pace and customer experience. A variety of dialing options ensures agents are working at the optimal pace for your campaign.
Single line, progressive, preview, and parallel dialers
Built into the sales engagement platform
Agents move through their calls faster and more efficiently 
[Learn more](https://vanillasoft.com/platform/auto-dialer-software)
![man talking on a headset with a pen in his hand](https://vanillasoft.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcdn.sanity.io%2Fimages%2Fc35pm3dk%2Fproduction%2F19d6ee94a3a06397be2ad37950634e4fadca4f92-1920x1080.jpg%3Fauto%3Dformat&w=3840&q=75)
###  Sales Automation
Vanillasoft’s sales automation tools orchestrate and automate outreach. We reduce agent busy work so your team can focus on conversations.
Automate calls and messages around the lead, one to one at scale
Lead management and auto dialing built in 
Increased agent activity and productivity
[Learn more](https://vanillasoft.com/platform/sales-automation)

We work across industries and workflows to deliver the best results — and fast-moving revenue teams with high value leads love us. Whether you work in Automotive Sales, Mortgage and Home Repair Services, or Merchant Services, fast-moving revenue teams will see Vanillasoft’s impact.

Facilitating easy agent onboarding and ramp-up.

Pushing the best record in real time, across multiple campaigns. 
Setting up fast, effective email and messaging sales process automation. 
Delivering powerful reporting and analytics.

Each contact was individually reviewed and prepared—a qualitative approach that was hardly scalable in operational terms, however, requiring around ten minutes of effort per lead. At the same time, the multi-channel strategy comprising LinkedIn, email, and telephone was run using several unconnected tools, which caused additional coordination effort. With Venta AI, Lotaro was able to automate personalized messaging for the first time with AI support and implement it in a scalable way. Individually prepared messages are now generated automatically, checked manually, and played out across channels – fully integrated into the HubSpot CRM. LinkedIn, email, and telephone are interlinked in a central workflow. The result: a 15% response rate, average cost per lead of around €150, and a time saving of around 90% compared to the manual process.](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/67ab5b2867f10e24e886e6af/698d829415387db885bcf472_lotarogruender.jpeg)](https://www.getventa.ai/)

**Is Venta AI GDPR-compliant?**
Yes, Venta AI is GDPR compliant. Our software is developed in the EU and hosted in Germany in compliance with the GDPR. Our AI employees can also access databases outside the EU, which are checked by us for their GDPR compliance. Further details can be found in our general terms and conditions.
**Can I also reach companies outside the EU with Venta AI?**
Yes, that is possible. Our AI employees have access to global databases and can conduct research in various languages. As our AI employees are trained in German and English, they are best suited for outreach in these languages.
**Which languages does Venta AI support?**
The Venta AI user interface currently supports German and English, but our AI SDR can also interpret information and generate messages in 80 other languages.
**We have special security requirements, can you fulfil them?**
We always endeavour to fulfil special requirements. Please get in touch with us to discuss details.
**What distinguishes you from a traditional lead agency?**
Venta AI is an AI employee for your team, which they configure and control 100% themselves.
**What does multi-channel outreach mean?**
Multi-channel outreach means contacting people on several channels, such as LinkedIn, email, telephone or by letter in a specific sequence. With Venta AI, it is possible to send messages directly by email, LinkedIn and letter and to find telephone numbers for contact by phone.

#  Vidu - the new Chinese text-to-video AI Model 
On 27th April 2024, [Tsinghua University](https://www.tsinghua.edu.cn/) and the Chinese AI startup [ShengShu Technology](https://www.shengshu-ai.com/) annouced "Vidu", a text-to-video AI model similar to OpenAI's [Sora](https://openai.com/sora). 
Unfortunately for us, they chose the name "Vidu" for their AI model. We've been using the name [VIDU](https://www.vidu.io/) for our product since 2021. 
NOTE: [VIDU](https://www.vidu.io/) is not the same as the recently announced Chinese text-to-video AI model also called "Vidu". 
We've detected that you're accessing this website from a county where we don't have existing customers, so we're blocking your access. 
Looking for text-to-video AI video generation?
[ 👉 Try text-to-video AI ](https://www.vidu.io/a/text-to-video)

## Turn Visitors Into Revenue
Drive more traffic and sales by setting up automation that triggers emails based on customer behavior from our platform. We’ll tell your email marketing system, CRM, Direct Mail, and Custom Audience platform who the prospect is, what pages they visited and how much time they spent. Then you can deliver personalized emails, direct mail, and custom audiences based on their buying behavior. Keep your brand front of mind until the point of purchase.
[START A FREE TRIAL](https://www.visualvisitor.com/sign-up/) [SCHEDULE A DEMO](https://www.visualvisitor.com/meet-product-specialist/)
### Show Me You Understand Me, And I'll Buy From You
The more data you have about your website visitors, the better you can communicate with them. Our platform provides data about your website visitors, including name, email, address, employment, income estimates, home ownership, product or service they are interested in, and many other data points. Use all of this to your advantage. Segment the data by elements essential to your business, and communicate.
  * Make it a two-way conversation.
  * Meet prospects on their terms
  * Connect about something meaningful


Show me you understand me, and I’ll buy from you.
[START A FREE TRIAL](https://www.visualvisitor.com/sign-up/) [SCHEDULE A DEMO](https://www.visualvisitor.com/meet-product-specialist/)
![3](https://www.visualvisitor.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/3.webp)
### Ridiculously Easy Way to Build Your Email List
**THE OLD WAY:** Building your email list can be painful and expensive. Drive traffic to your site, show an offer, and make sure your Call-to-Action converts. Even then, you only get a small portion of your website visitors.
**THE NEW WAY:** With WebID +Person, you can capture 35% of your website visitors by name, email, and even their visited pages. Then have this data automatically added to your Email List without lifting a finger.
![5](https://www.visualvisitor.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/5.png)
![6](https://www.visualvisitor.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/6.png)
### Reduce Your Paid Search Spend
If you now know who the visitor is and you have their email address, why pay to have them return? Instead, start an email dialogue with them. You’ll learn more about your prospects, understand where they are in the buying process, and keep your brand front of mind.
Increase the ROI of your digital advertising campaigns by following up with email and direct mail. Why pay for clicks that don’t convert? You can automatically trigger email, direct mail, social media, and/or display campaigns.

#### Optimize your trade show results
More sales – More conversions – More of everything..
[MORE INFORMATION](https://vivolead.com/opportunityapp/)
#  **VivoLead is a dynamic company specializing in providing comprehensive services,****knowledge, and digital products tailored to optimize sales value at trade shows or daily sales meetings.**
### Enhanced Lead Capture
With Vivolead’s intuitive lead capture solutions, exhibitors can effortlessly capture leads directly from the show floor. Our advanced scanning technology ensures accurate data capture, eliminating the hassle of manual entry and streamlining the lead qualification process. Say goodbye to missed opportunities and hello to actionable leads!
### Real-Time Engagement
Engage with prospects in real-time using Vivolead’s interactive engagement tools. From personalized surveys and quizzes to instant messaging and multimedia presentations, exhibitors can captivate attendees and create memorable interactions that resonate long after the event ends. Forge meaningful connections and convert leads into loyal customers with ease.
### Data-Driven Insights
Gain valuable insights into attendee behavior and preferences with Vivolead’s robust analytics platform. Track key metrics such as booth traffic, engagement levels, and lead quality to measure the success of your exhibiting efforts. Armed with actionable data, exhibitors can optimize their strategies, identify areas for improvement, and drive greater ROI.
### Seamless Integration
Vivolead seamlessly integrates with your existing CRM and marketing automation systems, ensuring seamless data transfer and eliminating silos between sales and marketing teams. Harness the power of unified data to nurture leads effectively, streamline follow-up processes, and accelerate the sales cycle.
### Customized Solutions
At Vivolead, we understand that every exhibitor is unique. That’s why we offer customizable solutions tailored to your specific needs and objectives. Whether you’re looking to generate qualified leads, increase brand visibility, or drive product sales, our team works closely with you to develop a personalized strategy that delivers results.
[MORE INFORMATION](https://vivolead.com/opportunityapp/)
### Cost and Time Savings
By leveraging Vivolead’s streamlined lead capture and engagement solutions, exhibitors can significantly reduce costs associated with manual lead retrieval and data entry. Our automated processes eliminate the need for paper-based forms and manual transcription, saving valuable time and resources that can be reallocated to more strategic activities.

## Before the Meeting
### Ava Knows the Room. You Own It.
Ava researches your account, gathers insights from CRM, email, and Slack, and creates quick-read stakeholder summaries and discovery prep so you know exactly who you're meeting and what matters most.
## During the Meeting
### An Expert at Your Side.
Ava joins your sales calls to listen, surface real-time insights, and instantly answer complex product or competitive questions so you can stay focused on the customer.
## After the Meeting
### Turn Every Conversation into Momentum.
Ava summarizes the discussion, drafts personalized follow-ups, and creates the next-step materials you need, like value cases, solution summaries, or sales handoff documents.

AI for Technical Sales - Sales Reasoning Model
POWERED BY AGENT INTELLIGENCE
## Sales Reasoning Model
Ava thinks like your top performers, using the Sales Reasoning Model to help reps strategize, sequence actions, and adapt to complex buying groups.
Ava knows how sales _actually_ works. She knows the difference between a champion and a buyer, understands how deals progress, and can connect insights across conversations—so she doesn't drift off-topic or give irrelevant advice like generic AI chatbots do.

## Privacy Preference Center
## Privacy Preference Center
  * ### Your Privacy
  * ### Strictly Necessary Cookies
  * ### Targeting Cookies
  * ### Performance Cookies
  * ### Functional Cookies
  * ### Social Media Cookies


#### Your Privacy
When you visit any website, it may store or retrieve information on your browser, mostly in the form of cookies. This information might be about you, your preferences or your device and is mostly used to make the site work as you expect it to. The information does not usually directly identify you, but it can give you a more personalized web experience. Because we respect your right to privacy, you can choose not to allow some types of cookies. Click on the different category headings to find out more and change our default settings. However, blocking some types of cookies may impact your experience of the site and the services we are able to offer.   
[More information.](https://www.vivun.com/cookie-list/)
#### Strictly Necessary Cookies
Always Active
These cookies are necessary for the website to function and cannot be switched off in our systems. They are usually only set in response to actions made by you which amount to a request for services, such as setting your privacy preferences, logging in or filling in forms. You can set your browser to block or alert you about these cookies, but some parts of the site will not then work. These cookies do not store any personally identifiable information.
Cookies Details‎
#### Targeting Cookies
Targeting Cookies
These cookies may be set through our site by our advertising partners. They may be used by those companies to build a profile of your interests and show you relevant adverts on other sites. They do not store directly personal information, but are based on uniquely identifying your browser and internet device. If you do not allow these cookies, you will experience less targeted advertising.
Cookies Details‎
#### Performance Cookies
Performance Cookies
These cookies allow us to count visits and traffic sources so we can measure and improve the performance of our site. They help us to know which pages are the most and least popular and see how visitors move around the site. All information these cookies collect is aggregated and therefore anonymous. If you do not allow these cookies we will not know when you have visited our site, and will not be able to monitor its performance.
Cookies Details‎
#### Functional Cookies
Functional Cookies
These cookies enable the website to provide enhanced functionality and personalisation. They may be set by us or by third party providers whose services we have added to our pages. If you do not allow these cookies then some or all of these services may not function properly.
Cookies Details‎
#### Social Media Cookies
Social Media Cookies
These cookies are set by a range of social media services that we have added to the site to enable you to share our content with your friends and networks. They are capable of tracking your browser across other sites and building up a profile of your interests. This may impact the content and messages you see on other websites you visit. If you do not allow these cookies you may not be able to use or see these sharing tools.
Cookies Details‎

Preferences Preferences

Statistics Statistics

# FiberAI
#### From Prospect to Customer in Seconds
## Intelligence for Every Stage
Scale your infrastructure business with AI that identifies opportunities, estimates costs, and manages customers in a single platform.

#### Quote
Instantly calculate monthly rates and one-time installation costs across your network and partner footprints.

#### Plan
Run high-level market feasibility studies or deep-dive into address-specific build costs and revenue potential.

#### Prospect
Surface high-value targets with complete contact intelligence and automated, professional proposals.

#### Service
Streamline post-sale operations with automated maintenance alerts and outage notifications for existing clients.
![FiberAI home](https://www.vizaport.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/Screenshot-2026-02-18-at-8.52.52-AM.png)
## The ROI of Intelligence
FiberAI isn’t just a tool; it’s a competitive advantage that eliminates manual bottlenecks and focuses your team on the deals that actually close.
[See Pricing](https://www.vizaport.com/fiberai-pricing/)
## Business Value
By shifting the burden of manual data analysis to AI, your team can pivot from administrative bottlenecks to high-impact growth initiatives.
##### High-Value Prospects
Stop chasing ZoomInfo leads that are not near your network. Pinpoint customers near your network and obtain high-quality contact information of potential buyers.
##### Faster Quote Time
In the race to provide quote requests, speed wins. Reduce response times from days to seconds, ensuring your proposal is the first one on the prospect’s desk.
##### Intelligent Planning
Remove the guesswork from capital expenditures. Use data-driven cost modeling to ensure every mile of fiber you build delivers maximum revenue.
## Reducing Sales Bottlenecks by 90%
Improving turnaround times allows key resources to focus on high-ROI deals.

# The easiest way to send an email campaign
Hit Compose in Gmail, enter your list, subject, and message.
[Add to Gmail](https://chrome.google.com/webstore/detail/gmass-powerful-mail-merge/ehomdgjhgmbidokdgicgmdiedadncbgf) GMass requires Chrome
5-star reviews from 300,000+ happy users
![Intro](https://cdn.gmass.co/assets/videos/intro.gif)
###  What can GMass do? 
  * Turn **Gmail** into an **email marketing** and **cold email platform**
  * Use **mail merge personalization** with **Google Sheets**
  * **Verify** your list, **test** links, & **fix spam** triggers before you send


  * Maximize your **deliverability** — **hit the inbox** , not the spam folder
  * Send **automated follow-up sequences**
  * **Break Gmail’s limits** — send virtually unlimited emails


####  Mail merge with Google Sheets 
Say goodbye to CSV files. Connect to Google Sheets to send a personalized mass email announcement or newsletter using any of the columns in your spreadsheet.
![Preview](https://cdn.gmass.co/assets/videos/video_1.gif)
####  Send cold emails 
The easiest way to send cold email sequences in Gmail.
![Preview](https://cdn.gmass.co/assets/videos/video_2.gif)
####  Build your list from existing contacts 
Use Gmail's powerful search feature to find messages containing recipients to whom you want to email. Then click the Build Email List button, and a Compose window will load containing the email addresses found in those messages. The only mass email service that does this!
![Preview](https://cdn.gmass.co/assets/videos/video_2.gif)
#### We send a lot of email. Watch these live stats grow right before your eyes.
Lifetime emails sent: 9,246,527,668   
Emails sent since midnight 2/20/2026: 1,695,063
[Join the party](https://chrome.google.com/webstore/detail/gmass-powerful-mail-merge/ehomdgjhgmbidokdgicgmdiedadncbgf) [See more stats](https://www.gmass.co/systemstatus)
### Features
![Break Gmail's Sending Limits](https://cdn.gmass.co/images/people.svg)
###### Mass Emails in Gmail
Our mass email service can break Gmail's sending limits using our distribution technology.
[More details](http://www.gmass.co/gmail-mass-email)
![Google Sheets Integration](https://cdn.gmass.co/images/sheet.svg)
###### Mail Merge with Google Sheets
GMass will read data live from any Google Sheet and even monitor for new rows and then send emails automatically.
[More details](https://www.gmass.co/features/google-sheets-integration)
![Reports](https://cdn.gmass.co/images/graph.svg)
###### Email Reporting Analytics
Campaign level reports that show how many people opened, clicked, replied, and bounced. See reports inside Gmail on your desktop or the Gmail app on your phone.
[More details](https://www.gmass.co/features/reporting)
![Personalization](https://cdn.gmass.co/images/personalization.svg)
###### Personalization
Personalize to your heart's content. Connect to a Google Sheet and personalize with any column, or use basic first and last name personalization without a spreadsheet. Use fallback values. Don't know someone's first name? We'll auto-detect it.
[More details](https://www.gmass.co/features/personalization-mass-emails)
![Automatic Follow-up Emails](https://cdn.gmass.co/images/clock.svg)
###### Automatic Follow-up Emails
Sending cold email? Set automatic follow-up emails to send in a sequence until your recipient replies. The best way to boost response rates.
[More details](https://www.gmass.co/features/auto-follow-up-gmail)
![Scheduling](https://cdn.gmass.co/images/calendar.svg)
###### Schedule Mass emails and Mail Merges
Schedule a mail merge for any time in the future, or set it to repeat daily or hourly.
[More details](https://www.gmass.co/features/gmail-scheduling)
![Manual Follow-up Campaigns](https://cdn.gmass.co/images/forward.svg)
###### Behavior-based Campaigns
Send to a segment of a prior campaign, like everyone who opened the last campaign, or everyone who didn't click the last campaign.
[More details](http://www.gmass.co/blog/new-feature-send-follow-up-mail-merge-campaigns-in-gmail/)
![Reply Management](https://cdn.gmass.co/images/management.svg)
###### Reply Management
Emails received in response to a mass email, including replies and bounces, are automatically categorized for you, preventing Inbox clutter.
[More details](https://www.gmass.co/features/reply-management)
![Email List Builder](https://cdn.gmass.co/images/email2.svg)
###### Email List Builder
Find email addresses deep inside your Gmail account just by searching.
[More details](https://www.gmass.co/features/gmail-list-builder)
[Add GMass Extension to Gmail](https://chrome.google.com/webstore/detail/gmass-powerful-mail-merge/ehomdgjhgmbidokdgicgmdiedadncbgf) GMass requires Chrome

Here's [why GMass is better.](https://www.gmass.co/blog/what-makes-gmass-better/)

#  **One-stop solution for**  
**Mobile Sales Execution**
On XSales℠ our Suite provides all functions & features to boost your field force performance, improve customer satisfaction and reach your most ambitious
revenue goals.
[Learn more](https://xsalesmobility.com/es/products/ "Suite")
## **Key Benefits**
We optimize the four key aspects that drive any Business growth and impact brand awareness & recognition.
###### Increase Sales & Revenue
We improve every stage of the sales cycle, generating more sales, exceeding quotas & growing the installed client’s base.
###### Improve Customer Satisfaction
Standarize your sales process acrross all channels and players, to provide better services & experiences.
![XSales® Mobility](https://xsalesmobility.com/wp-content/uploads/sites/6/2021/08/MicrosoftTeams-image-5.png)
[Why choosing us](https://xsalesmobility.com/home/why-choosing-us/ "Suite")
###### Improve Operational Efficiency
We automate all manual processes and create a consistent data flow between the back-end and the field.
###### Enhance Management capabilities
We empower your Supervisors to get total visibility over their sales teams activity and improve decision making.
## **Our Suite**
We provide top mobile workforce & sales management solutions  
to make sales simpler, smarter and more productive at all levels and under any market situation.
![](https://xsalesmobility.com/wp-content/uploads/sites/6/2024/12/dispositivo-SFA.png)
#### [XSales℠ SFA](https://xsalessfa.com/)
Empower your sales reps with an end-to-end solution that covers the entire sales cycle and integrates directly to your ERP.
![](https://xsalesmobility.com/wp-content/uploads/sites/6/2024/12/Consumer.png)
#### [XSales℠ Consumer](https://xsalesconsumer.com/)
Allow your customers to place pre-orders directly from suppliers through a self-service platform that works 100% remotely. 
![](https://xsalesmobility.com/wp-content/uploads/sites/6/2024/12/Maps-1.png)
#### [XSales℠ Maps](https://xsalesmaps.com/)
Get a GPS map visualization of all your mobile work forces & points of interest, and configure alerts to track pain points. 
![](https://xsalesmobility.com/wp-content/uploads/sites/6/2024/12/Store-4.png)
#### [XSales℠ Store](https://xsalesstore.com/)
Distribute all your Android corporate applications and configure massive updates and deployments through role-based access. 
[Learn more](https://xsalesmobility.com/es/products/ "Suite")

Follow our guide
### Solutions
Give your sales organization and prospects the benefit of a guided selling operational team. Each Zebrafi module is part of an overall strategy the Zebrafi team uses to guide your team to the prospects and customers where your solution delivers the most value. 
[ ](https://zebrafi.com/scoring/)
#### [Ideal Customer Profile](https://zebrafi.com/scoring/)
Zebrafi talks with customers and builds an initial Ideal Customer Profile (ICP) with the executive team. The ICP is put in front of the sales team and refined with their feedback. Bi-weekly meetings to discuss real opportunities and use the ICP to move the deals forward. Resources such as solution and demonstration experts, access to R&D, sales and executive management is now based on a measurable prioritization process
[ Learn More ](https://zebrafi.com/scoring/)
[ ](https://zebrafi.com/voc)
#### [Voice of the Customer](https://zebrafi.com/voc)
Zebrafi talks with your customers and builds Voice of the Customer (VOC) assets. VoC's organize **and** quantify all the ways your solution creates value. Bi-weekly sales meetings discuss new deals and reinforces metrics from case studies. Zebrafi guides reps and brings transparency for reps to talk about previous strategic deals as if they had closed them.
[ Learn more ](https://zebrafi.com/voc)
[ ](https://zebrafi.com/value-story)
#### [Value Story](https://zebrafi.com/value-story/)
Budget tightening and group buying has increased the need for a business case. The Zebrafi team talks with your customers and identifies critical value drivers for the sales team to address on opportunities. It includes total cost of ownership or ROI and leans heavy on how the value was delivered to existing customers? Zebrafi trains your account executives how to build a collaborative Value Story with prospects. No more outrageous ROI messaging. Its rooted in bringing transparency to how the value is created.
[ learn more ](https://zebrafi.com/value-story)
[ ](https://zebrafi.com/retention/)
#### [Retention](https://zebrafi.com/retention/)
Are you waiting until renewal before engaging with your customer? Zebrafi will prepare your team to leverage the Value Story that was created for strategic accounts for a productive retention meeting post sale.
[ learn more ](https://zebrafi.com/retention/)
#### Sales Chat
Preparing for a weekly sales meeting? Use Natural Language and AI to ask questions about the sales data that lives inside of Zebrafi. Example: "Show Opportunities where the Zebra Score was modified this week"
[ Sales Chat ](https://zebrafi.com/salesbot/)
#### Can we join your Team?
Ongoing coaching, mentoring, education and change management along with the development of marketing collateral and materials creation
[ Contact Us ](https://zebrafi.com/#contact)
### Traditional Pipeline
Close Rate
15%
Right now, you’re most likely using a traditional sales pipeline. Unfortunately, because you’re not able to prioritize one deal over another, your sales pipeline probably contains very few “really good” prospects.
### Zebrafi Pipeline
Close rate
90%
Zebrafi makes sure that only qualified deals get pursued. Once your sales pipeline is filled with _**Zebras**_ , you’ve got the visibility to see the status of every active deal.

Playbooks flatten it.

## Understanding why you win — and lose — is what makes success repeatable.
![Zime GTM Sales Brain - Learning how your team wins and turning it into action](https://zime.ai/images/homepage-images/sales-brain.jpg)
_check_circle_ Converts unstructured GTM knowledge into behaviors
_check_circle_ Model winning behaviors with historical won & lost deals
_check_circle_ Builds behavioral cues such as hesitation vs commitment. Helps qualify voice of customer

## Frequently asked questions
##### Is your lead database compliant with data privacy laws?
Yes, our data is collected in compliance with global data privacy laws, including GDPR and CCPA ensuring secure and ethical data usage.
##### How frequently is the data updated?
Our contact information and buyer insights are continually refreshed through automated systems, ensuring that you have access to the most current and relevant data.
##### How can buyer personality insights help accelerate my sales process?
Personality insights provide valuable data on a prospect's preferences, communication style, motivators, and decision-making behaviour, allowing you to tailor your sales approach for improved engagement.
##### How accurate is your contact information?
Our contact information on an average is more than 95% accurate.
##### Can Zintlr chrome extension be used only on LinkedIn?
No, Zintlr chrome extension can be used to discover contact information on LinkedIn, Zauba Corp, and any other website.

## Your privacy is our responsibility
We believe that trust is paramount in a relationship. We do not own or sell your data, and we most certainly do not bank on advertising-based business models. The only way we make money is from the software license fees you pay us.
Watch Video
![Core-value-banner](data:image/svg+xml;charset=utf8,%3Csvg%20xmlns%3D%22http%3A%2F%2Fwww.w3.org%2F2000%2Fsvg%22%20viewBox%3D%22100%25%20100%25%20200%20150%22%3E%3C%2Fsvg%3E)
## The core values and principles that drive us
### Long-term commitment
30+ years of running a profitable organization gives us a good sense of challenges that a growing business faces. We take pride in running a sustainable business that’s powered by you, our customer.
### Focus on research and development
Software is our craft and we back it up with our relentless investments in R&D. So much so that we prefer to own the entire technology stack, including running our data centers globally.
### Customer-first philosophy
In all these years, it's our customers' trust and goodwill that has helped us establish a strong position in the market. No matter the size of your business, we're here to help you grow.
[Read our story](https://www.zoho.com/ourstory.html?src=zindex)
#### Transnational Localism
"Zoho follows a long-term approach, and therefore, our growth will be rooted in closely working with and serving the local communities while staying connected through shared knowledge and culture. A strong local presence will help us in effectively addressing the needs of local businesses and add a personal touch to our services."

### [The Ultimate Guide to LinkedIn Sales Navigator: A Manual for B2B Sales Success - Part IV](https://www.dealcode.ai/blog/the-ultimate-guide-to-linkedin-sales-navigator-a-manual-for-b2b-sales-success-part-iv)
The crucial lever for scaling sales success lies in activating the entire company network. Without team features, every sales representative operates in a silo. With the TeamLink feature—the primary reason for upgrading to a team plan—your company's collective network becomes a searchable, strategic asset. The feature digitally answers the key question of every sales meeting: "Who knows someone at our target account?". It identifies warm introduction paths through colleagues and transforms cold outreach into trust-based initial contacts. This fundamentally increases the entire team's efficiency and success rate, justifying the investment in a collaborative platform.

### [The Ultimate Guide to LinkedIn Sales Navigator: A Manual for B2B Sales Success - Part III](https://www.dealcode.ai/blog/the-ultimate-guide-to-linkedin-sales-navigator-a-manual-for-b2b-sales-success-part-iii)
To maximize sales efficiency, distinguish between Sales Navigator's AI buying signals. Buyer Intent shows concrete interest in your company and is a direct cue for sales to act immediately. Product Category Intent indicates general interest in a solution type, creating an opportunity for marketing to build trust with content. This strategic separation prevents premature sales pitches and focuses your most valuable resources on accounts that are ready to close.

The feature digitally answers the key question of every sales meeting: "Who knows someone at our target account?". It identifies warm introduction paths through colleagues and transforms cold outreach into trust-based initial contacts. This fundamentally increases the entire team's efficiency and success rate, justifying the investment in a collaborative platform.
